  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b24cf27f-68c9-412a-9cb7-3723f0c67d2f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/25771940-jemma-dinsey">Jemma Dinsey</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Honestly I got tired reading this book. I was so filled with anticipation from the first book so was hoping for something great somewhere in the book.<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Honestly I got tired reading this book. I was so filled with anticipation from the first book so was hoping for something great somewhere in the book...<br />Dragged myself through it an had to stop somewhere in the middle. I'm disappointed .<br />It kept repeating the same things and actions and emotions over and over and over with nothing new. Had to keep asking myself if it was the same author who wrote the first book, I'm definitely not going to try the third one.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<div id="review_429093099" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429093099" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429093099?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429093099" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6276478622065835744">Spoiler-free review!<br/><br/><i> <b> “I promise you, I will pick up every broken piece of you, every single fucking piece, Grace, and for the rest of my fucking life, I will put you back together… I’ll make you whole again.“ </b></i> <br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757629._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was a bumpy ride that had me screaming “WTF!!” in frustration at my kindle on more than one occasion but had me swooning so freaking hard over Shane that I just couldn’t put it down!!<br/><br/>I read it in one sitting. I was exhausted but it kept me glued to my Kindle until 3am just flipp</span>
  <span id="freeText6276478622065835744" style="display:none">Spoiler-free review!<br><br><i> <b> “I promise you, I will pick up every broken piece of you, every single fucking piece, Grace, and for the rest of my fucking life, I will put you back together… I’ll make you whole again.“ </b></i> <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757629._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was a bumpy ride that had me screaming “WTF!!” in frustration at my kindle on more than one occasion but had me swooning so freaking hard over Shane that I just couldn’t put it down!!<br><br>I read it in one sitting. I was exhausted but it kept me glued to my Kindle until 3am just flipping the pages!<br><br>This sequel to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15768536.Fall_From_Grace__Mad_World___1_" title="Fall From Grace (Mad World, #1) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Fall From Grace</a> picks up right where that insane cliffhanger from book 1 ended and because of all the twists in this story, I’m actually not going to say a single word about the plot and I’d highly suggest you not look up anything about it. If the premise of book 1 intrigues you then this one won’t disappoint.<br><br>I did really like that after the paranormal intensity of the ending of book 1, this book took a bit of a step back and allowed the character development to take over for while before building back up to the heavier paranormal part.<br><br>This isn’t quite the kind of book I normally go for because there was a lot of back and forth between Shane and Grace- a lot of “are they” or “aren’t they” and “will they” or “won’t they”, and at the start of this one, I honestly wasn’t sure where the story was really going but because the intense sexual tension was just off the freaking charts and oh-so-swoony, and I was laughing, enjoying myself, and occasionally clutching at my heart, I basically let go and just went with it.<br><br>It did however lead me ask about a million questions – Who was… ? How did…? But if [important event] happened like this, then doesn’t it mean that….? Is he still…? WHY WOULD HE….? When did she….? What was he thinking when he….? and it went on and on and on…<br><br>There were a few situations that pushed me to the very brinks of my frustration limits (to. the. brink) - seriously there were times when I questioned if they were going to make it relationship-wise, but holy SWOON, once I got to the end, I was in heaven. (no pun, honestly, I swear)<br><br><i> <b> ”…just stay with me. I need you like I fucking need to breathe.” </b></i> <br><br>Shane Shane freaking Shane Maxton… the tattooed man-whore rock god. Oh the swoon, the heart ache, then more swoon, and more heartache… and then even more epic freaking swoon!!! I totally LOVED him, I wanted to throttle him, I wanted to hug him, I wanted to geld him, and I totally wanted to do other things to him that I won’t go into right now *winks*<br><br><i> <b> “Dear God, there is just something about this man that makes you want to stick your panties in his pockets and tell him you’re half way there…” </b></i>  &lt;— *nods* yeah, pretty much.<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385743i/744819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything about Shane and Grace is just so intense! For most of the book, they were either fighting or kissing. There isn’t a whole ton of actual sex in this book until the end but with all the music playing (<i> “Come on, girl, play with me.” </i> *swooooon*), serious UST and eye fucking going on, you really don’t miss it!!<br><br><i> “I think I could have had an orgasm from the mind fuck he was giving me right there.” </i><br><br>I do wish they could have communicated more because I feel like that would have solved like 90% of their issues but at the same time, I enjoyed the bumpy ride of this story so much that even though that’s normally really important to me in stories, I really just kind of accepted it here as character quirks.<br><br>And that the ending was gorgeously swoony and I was so glad to finally see them get their HEA!! At the end, when he… hmm, I won’t say what he did, but when he did <i> that thing </i> (and get your minds out of the gutters now, it has nothing to do with <i> that </i>... yeesh), I totally teared up and got chills. It was AMAZING and romantic and heart melting!!!<br><br>But! I have to say that if I were to have one complaint about this book its that I found some of Shane’s behavior frustrating to the point of going a little too far. Sigh. My heart really, realllly hurt and I still don’t understand why he did some of the things he did especially knowing what I know about the ending. Grace and Shane always had a bit of an intense, totally-undeniably-drawn-to-each-other relationship and yet at the same time they were really dysfunctional – which I was able to look past for the most part because of the raging chemistry they had going on but I felt that there were two times when Shane took things just too far in ways that could have been easily avoidable and, because this book was only told from Grace’s POV, I found those times made me kinda of fall out of love with him a little – or at least, just so unable to understand his actions that it pushed me away from him… And there were a few questions that I found were still unanswered about the whole story as a whole in regards to him. BUT, I hear that the author is writing either the next book or a whole collection of scenes from his POV so I’m really hoping that after reading those, I’ll understand his actions more and come to terms with those scenes because I really, truly fell HARD for him. Seriously, he totally worked his way into my heart &lt;3<br><br><i> <b> “Look Gray… A decent guy doesn’t just get born and grow up to be Mr. Perfect. They need to be created by a woman. They’re like a dumb blank lump of clay and you have to mold them into what you want them to be, while erasing everything their mothers ever taught them and all the horrible Internet porn they’ve watched growing up.” </b></i> <br><br>If you want a fun contemporary romance about soul-mates with a unique paranormal twist and a HEA, then you’ll probably really love these!<br><br>And at $1.50 each from Amazon, you really should grab yourselves copies and meet the delicious HOTNESS that is Shane Maxton &lt;3<br><br>CASTING (above and below)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385743i/744820._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757630._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6276478622065835744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer643253318" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7168091933501387786"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849646.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849647.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>Blacky</b> - a young woman in search of the book of her life<br/><b>Savingrace</b> - uber-hot and famous book, separated from Blacky for months, a tortured soul disappointed in life<br/><b>Evildude</b> - the bad guy, no explanation necessary<br/><br/><br/><b>*written from Blacky's POV*</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849648.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Once upon a time existed a book. Fall from Grace was the name.<br/>Legend says it had a really, really hot guy in it.<br/>His name was whispered in the shadows and passed through generations of horny teens as a sex symbol.<br/>The story and romance were rumored to be amazing</span>
  <span id="freeText7168091933501387786" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849646.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849647.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Blacky</b> - a young woman in search of the book of her life<br><b>Savingrace</b> - uber-hot and famous book, separated from Blacky for months, a tortured soul disappointed in life<br><b>Evildude</b> - the bad guy, no explanation necessary<br><br><br><b>*written from Blacky's POV*</b><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849648.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Once upon a time existed a book. Fall from Grace was the name.<br>Legend says it had a really, really hot guy in it.<br>His name was whispered in the shadows and passed through generations of horny teens as a sex symbol.<br>The story and romance were rumored to be amazing, set in a paranormal world, with main characters as fallen angels.<br>Wanna know how I know all this?<br>I was one of the people who actually read that book.<br>And I am here to tell you the story of how I found the sequel, and what that book put me through...<br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849649.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I found myself trapped in a heavenly library by Evildude who is set on separating me from my one true book soul mate, Savingrace.<br><br>"You will never read that book, Blacky! I burn for you, we are meant to be together!!," roared Evildude with an evil glint in his evil eyes!<br><br>I got in his face and screamed with all my fury at him, "NEVER! My soul may be bleeding and my heart may be crushed and splintered into a billion little pieces but I am strong enough to defy you! I will save all my love for Savingrace, so back off, moron!"<br><br>Evildude turned his evil eyes at me. I could tell he was being in an evil mood because of his squinting.<br>Damn. He is gonna talk some more.<br><br>"I have waited for you for ages Blacky. You don't understand my passion for you Blacky. Yes, I obviously have to repeat your name in every sentence because you are too stupid to figure out who I'm talking to, BLACKY." He turned away from me and I saw him shaking. <br>"Mwahahahahaha", he evil laughed at me.<br>"I will destroy your Savingrace and even you if I have to! If I can't have you, no book will!"<br><br>With that, Evildude turned around and left me staring at a wall, thinking of my Savingrace and feeling my heart splinter again into a billion little pieces and my poor soul bleed again until I was left completely emotionally ruined.<br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849650.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I woke up sitting at a library, surrounded by thousands of books and with my mind full of confusion.<br>Why did Evildude want me? I just couldn't understand it.<br>I couldn't stop thinking of finding my Savingrace, but then, I couldn't stop feeling hurt by Savingrace either.<br>After all this time searching for each other, Savingrace obviously didn't feel the same as I do. I felt betrayed. My heart broke because my love for Savingrace was not returned.<br>I'd decided to hate Savingrace for not wanting to be read by me with the same force as I wanted to read it.<br><br>After a couple of hours of thinking about the subject, I decided to move on and read other books. Why save myself for my one and only book, if that book doesn't feel the same about me?<br><br>Off I went, looking through the covers and blurbs, trying to find something interesting.<br><br>That was when it happened.<br><br>I saw Savingrace tucked in the wrong shelf, surrounded by books of the wrong genre.<br>It must have been torture.<br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849651.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Even though I now had my Savingrace, I could not let go of my anger and betrayal enough to read it. <br>My poor bleeding soul and broken heart just couldn't allow me to get past the fact that Savingrace did nothing to somehow get to me. It's not that I'm unreasonable but seriously, do I have to do everything????<br><br>And so I went to my living room to look at my book, because even though I couldn't read it, I was happy to know it was there and it was AMAZING to look at. I mean FANTASIC!!<br><br>Anyway, the first thing I saw was a friend of mine, holding Savingrace. And reading it!<br><br>"What are you doing?," I screamed while my heart was being torn from my chest and completely stepped upon until it was totally dead and not beating anymore but I somehow managed to magically survive the ordeal.<br><br>"How could you do this to me?," I whispered while cold tears went down my cheeks to show I was incredibly sad and heartbroken.<br>"I thought we had something special, and you are letting someone else read you!," I screamed at my book. Yes, I really love screaming at everything.<br><br>I could see the book was trying to explain but I didn't want to hear it!<br><br>I have the right to get angry at someone for not having any choice to control a situation, and I have every right to not listen to any explanations and stay completely angry at that person till the end of time!<br><br>Savingrace was torn by my outburst, I could see it, but at that point I didn't really care. There are other books to read.<br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849652.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Even though I decided I would never forgive Savingrace for letting anyone else read it, I still couldn't stop thinking about the damn book.<br>Maybe I was wrong. Maybe the book really couldn't help it!<br>I grabbed my backpack and ran home so I could talk to Savingrace ASAP!<br><br>I was so excited that I didn't see my huge bookshelf when I was entering my living room, and I ran right into it.<br>That left me covered with books, and with Savingrace standing on my desk, with a look full of rage and betrayal, and heartbreak and a whole rainbow of emotions that are very difficult to explain.<br><br>"I... No, it isn't what you think...," I uselessly tried to get out of the situation, but to no avail. Savingrace was uber-angry, I could feel it's rage across the room.<br><br>It made my heart burst from my chest and shatter into another million pieces, and pain blossomed in my chest because it all felt SO BAD!!!<br><br>Savingrace shut her pages and turned from me.<br>It broke my heart all over again.<br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849653.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>And so, after another ten or so situations where either myself or Savingrace completely overreacted and screamed a bit at each other, and of course I forgot all the tension between us, the wanting-to-read-but-can't situation, we decided to try it out, and see how it goes.<br>Only, our bliss was interrupted by Evildude!!!<br><br>BUT! <br><br>I will not tell you what happened. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849654.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425651i/849655.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Well, I got my happy ever after with Savingrace, having finally read it, but then after being so irritated by the characters I simply could not love it like I thought I would.<br>It was just not meant to be.<br><br>But then, I have heard whispers...<br>I feel it in the water...<br>I feel it in the earth...<br>I smell it in the air...<br><br><br>Shane's book exists!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12385358523108801370"><b>4+ Fallen Angels, Endless Love, Alcohol and Bad Boy Rock - Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415489ra/820133.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the beginning of time, before the world becomes old, God was merciful and vengeful, at the same time and angels were still pure. A small band of them was stationed on Earth to help the humans, but they were corrupted. They fell in love with the women and they gave birth to abominations. The giants, the Nephelim. There were no other choice. God punished them. They fell from grace and they were imprisoned in hell. And their human w</span>
  <span id="freeText12385358523108801370" style="display:none"><b>4+ Fallen Angels, Endless Love, Alcohol and Bad Boy Rock - Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415489ra/820133.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the beginning of time, before the world becomes old, God was merciful and vengeful, at the same time and angels were still pure. A small band of them was stationed on Earth to help the humans, but they were corrupted. They fell in love with the women and they gave birth to abominations. The giants, the Nephelim. There were no other choice. God punished them. They fell from grace and they were imprisoned in hell. And their human women were punished along them. But, there was a couple that was pure. Shamsiel and Selah. Their only crime? A single kiss, that doomed them for all eternity. Selah never got to die. She became a lost soul, cursed to live in the empty shells that people left behind, forced to look for a pair of warm blue eyes throughout eternity. And left Shamsiel falling from Grace only to find her all over again when they were both on the brink of giving up forever.<br><br><i>
  <b>“It is a pure soul who can hold true the innocence and timelessness of passion in another soul. Each unveiling the greatest pieces of the other, locked together at the heart for eternity.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426862i/853265.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Grace realized what her heart has been screaming at her from the beginning. Shane is her angel, the one she spent eternity looking for. But she realized it after having both their hearts broken and she ended up in a coma with her soul held hostage by a vindictive angel, with his own agenda that spent the last 2000 years pretending to help her.<br><br>She will find her way back but not to Shane’ arms. Eons of misconceptions, miscommunication, lack of trust and so much love that ultimately broke them, will keep them apart once again. Two hardheaded individuals who end up hurting each other with every word and gesture, but unable to deny their overwhelming feelings. <br><br><i>
  <b>“ I guess I didn’t know him like I thought I did and he destroyed my heart. But he didn’t just destroy a small piece of my heart, he desecrated the whole thing. I was the idiot who just handed it to him. Because for so long, I really, really believed...I had faith in him, but I was wrong.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372318ra/725579.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Love can’t be denied for long and after lots of booze, shoes and bad boys with tattoos, just about when we are going to die from severe sexual tension and our frustration reaches new levels, HALLELUJAH! We are rewarded with the most anticipated sex scene ever after Mr. Darcy and Elizabeth’s kiss in “Pride &amp; Prejudice”. Seriously guys, I almost died waiting for you to consummate...<br><br><i>
  <b>” Let me in, because I promise you, I will pick up every little broken piece of you, every single fucking piece, Grace, and for the rest of my fucking life I will put you back together...I’ll make you whole again.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417067ra/824491.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426862ra/853266.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/655028.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405591ra/790362.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>AND THEN... FINALLY!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426862ra/853267.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lacking the haunting atmosphere of the first but more hip, funny and suspenseful, this second book frustrates and hooks you and you are unable to tear your eyes off the Shane the Magnificent,<br><br><i>
  <b> “Perfection. He was utterly the most breathtaking, painfully beautiful man I had ever laid my eyes on.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426862ra/853268.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Grace the Determined and their merry band of friends, desperately trying to find their way back to each other…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>♪♫ I didn’t know I was lost <br>Until you found me <br>I never knew what love was <br>Until you touched my hand <br>I lost myself long ago In between your lips <br>And now here you are <br>You steal my breath away <br>Until you I never really knew heaven<br>Cause until you it was only ever hell <br>I didn’t know I was so far gone <br>Until you brought me home <br>I promise you, girl I know you’re shattered<br>I’ll pick up your pieces <br>And make you whole again <br>Cause until you girl I’ve been shattered too <br>Since my very first kiss <br>It’s only been you ♪♫</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/475397.gif" width="400" height="212" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now for the most anticipated male POV… Shane, love, I am in for a wild ride!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426862ra/853269.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426862ra/853270.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2291340903" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2291340903" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2291340903?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=fallen-angels">fallen-angels</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2291340903" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2021609219944961059">First I want to say that I loved some of C. Zolendz’s books more than I can explain but this paranormal series of hers hugely disappointed me, unfortunately.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467343666ra/19581475.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There was an interesting enough plot – but the execution of it was not good and it became a torture for me to finish reading these two books.<br/><br/>If I need to compare, Book 1 is a bit better than Book 2, and honestly, I could have given it 3 stars if the second book were 4 or 5-star worthy, but alas, Book 2 killed it all! <br/><br/>Now, the whole series is</span>
  <span id="freeText2021609219944961059" style="display:none">First I want to say that I loved some of C. Zolendz’s books more than I can explain but this paranormal series of hers hugely disappointed me, unfortunately.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467343666ra/19581475.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was an interesting enough plot – but the execution of it was not good and it became a torture for me to finish reading these two books.<br><br>If I need to compare, Book 1 is a bit better than Book 2, and honestly, I could have given it 3 stars if the second book were 4 or 5-star worthy, but alas, Book 2 killed it all! <br><br>Now, the whole series is max 2 or 2,5 stars for me.<br><br><b>The plot:</b><br><br>Thousands of years ago, some of the angels sent to watch the humans for their safety fell in love with the beauty of the human women and those angels took them as wives and created the offsprings called the Nephilim but they turned out to be savage giants. <br><br>That’s why, the angels sent to watch the humans were punished – they were fallen. One of the human women who only had a heavenly kiss but nothing more with one of these angels was punished to live the rest of her eternity as a lost soul in search of the fallen angel that she loves.<br><br>And she is our heroine in this series. In this life and body she comes into, she is called Grace. And in this life, she is supposed to meet her soul mate angel. (The angel called Gabriel, who sometimes appears and guides her tells her that bit of information).<br><br>Grace meets a man-whore rock star in this life. Shane is immediately attracted to Grace and she is to him. <br><br><b>The whole of the two books in the series go as annoying as follows:</b><br><br>Grace finds Shane hot and irresistible but he is a man-whore and when he is saying he loves her, he can’t mean that, can he?<br><br>And Grace needs to find her soul mate angel and this man-whore can’t be him so she goes out with the wrong guys, assuming one of them is her fallen angel. <br><br>Being jealous and angry, Shane kisses groupies in front of her, acting like a d*ckhead. <br><br>All along the two books, there is this stupid “teen drama” between twenty-something-year old adults. <br><br>She wants him but she doesn’t want to want him. Although everybody else sees he has feelings for her, she insists that after one- night stand, he will move on to the next girl, so there is this ongoing and frustrating pull and push between them. <br><br>There is nothing more than a kiss or some hot and intense staring between the two of them until the last chapters of Book 2. <br><br>And at a certain point, I just stopped caring if they would be together or not, I just wanted to be out of their story asap. <br><br>They were like stupid 15-year old teens all the time. They just cannot communicate!!<br><br>For example, when she sees a woman beside him, she immediately assumes that he has slept with her. <br><br>He is not more mature than her, either. He assumes she slept with his friend when he sees her getting out of his bedroom. He doesn’t even ask properly why she was there and what they were doing. <br><br>It is like watching “two spoiled teens” blaming each other all the time about being with other people. I was yelling all the time, saying "Oh, please f*cking learn to communicate and please behave like adults!" But of course, in vain!<br><br>There are those rare moments when they get a little bit close and intimate, trusting each other's feelings a little bit more but every time, something happens so that they cannot go any further than kissing and touching. It is so frustrating, it is like the bad soap opera episodes where they stretch the happy end for months or years, all the while creating stupid drama.<br><br>The fallen angels, the devil and the good angels sometimes appear and add some paranormal sh*t into the mix and not all of it makes sense. And the fist fight of angels was the most absurd of all!<br><br>All in all, I can only appreciate the idea behind it, as the plot was interesting but the execution of it was more than annoying and boring.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518308613ra/25038636.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am really sorry to give a “Christine Zolendz book” a low rating but it can’t be helped, unfortunately…</span>
  <a data-text-id="2021609219944961059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_438138276" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/438138276" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/438138276?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=rockers">rockers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pnr-angels-demons">pnr-angels-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer438138276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3470530724229131928">So, after finishing book 1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15768536.Fall_From_Grace__Mad_World___1_' title='Fall From Grace (Mad World, #1) by Christine Zolendz' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fall From Grace</a> at 3am this morning, and absolutely loving it, I got 5 hours sleep and was then straight into this one. Was it worth it – <b>HELL YEAH!!!</b><br/><br/>It picks up immediately after the hideous cliffhanger of book 1 (thank God!) with Grace dealing with fallout from that big, dramatic climax. I’m not going to go into detail about the storyline because I don’t want to give any kind of spoiler. The story is amazing, but intense, and best experienced just to read and feel it</span>
  <span id="freeText3470530724229131928" style="display:none">So, after finishing book 1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15768536.Fall_From_Grace__Mad_World___1_" title="Fall From Grace (Mad World, #1) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Fall From Grace</a> at 3am this morning, and absolutely loving it, I got 5 hours sleep and was then straight into this one. Was it worth it – <b>HELL YEAH!!!</b><br /><br />It picks up immediately after the hideous cliffhanger of book 1 (thank God!) with Grace dealing with fallout from that big, dramatic climax. I’m not going to go into detail about the storyline because I don’t want to give any kind of spoiler. The story is amazing, but intense, and best experienced just to read and feel it all as you go – my emotions were all over the place! I will just say that there is a HEA, but there are many twists and turns along the way. <br /><br />I love these characters! Grace is amazing, even more so than she was in the first book, Lea is hilarious, with some absolutely brilliant dialogue, and the guys from the band are all back in their rude, crude yet affectionate glory. The way they all come together like a family and have each other’s backs is gorgeous. And of course there’s Shane *dreamy sigh*. I had a mad case of insta-love with Shane in book 1, but I fell deeper for him in this one. There’s nothing quite like a reformed, man-whorish bad boy who has fallen hard for his girl, but it’s all a bit deeper and more intense now, and oh my God is he freaking SWOONY!!!<br /><br />I will admit that some of the to-and-fro stuff that happened between Grace and Shane in the middle of the book did get annoying, and I was wondering whether we'd ever get to see them happy together. I just wanted to smack their heads together and tell them to get on with it! But there was SOOOOO must sexual tension and enough beautiful moments between them (loved the use of music in this <i>"'Come on, girl, play with me', he whispered"</i>) to keep us die-hard romantics happy amidst the confusion and the heart wrenching scenes as they almost tore each other apart:<br /><br /><i>“Just pull the fucking trigger on me now, </i>please.” <br /><br />*sob* But oh God, it was worth all of the heartache for the incredible, utterly epic, swoony resolution. And it wasn’t just one scene – it went on and on, and it was absolutely magic!<br /><br /><i>“I wanted to tell you how I felt. Why I was always so mean to you, Shane. ”<br />“Because you feel broken?”<br />“Completely shattered,” I whispered softly.<br />…<br />Bringing his hands to my face, he leaned over me, lightly stroking my cheeks with his fingertips. “Then let me in, because I promise you, I will pick up every little broken piece of you, every single fucking piece, Grace, and for the rest of my fucking life I will put you back together…I’ll make you whole again.” </i><br /><br />HOLY FREAKING SWOOOOOOOOOOOOOON!!! And some seriously steamy hotness too. Absolute perfection!<br /><br />The bad guy is evil and creepy, and the paranormal element is a unique one (well at least to me), and has enough of a mystery about it to keep you guessing what’s actually going on until the very end. But it’s the deep connection of soul mates and lovers that is the real focus of the series, and it’s done brilliantly! <br /><br />The perfect blend of romance, humour and angst, my heart was pounding through pretty much all of this book - both books actually, and I absolutely could not put either of them down. I'm flying high from the ending, and probably won't come down for days!<br /><br />I can't wait to get my hands on Shane’s story. <br /><br />5 epic stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3470530724229131928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654888830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6498837535132674552">As busy as I was this weekend, I devoured this book quite quickly! Once again, I have thoroughly enjoyed the blossoming romance of Shane and Grace. This book had sizzle, the sexual tension was intense and at times heartwrenching and frustrating. I love every minute of it though, and when these two get together-they cause the earth to move. I kid you not, this book had some of the most erotic scenes in it that I have ever read. All, I will tell you about one scene in particular is that Grace scre</span>
  <span id="freeText6498837535132674552" style="display:none">As busy as I was this weekend, I devoured this book quite quickly! Once again, I have thoroughly enjoyed the blossoming romance of Shane and Grace. This book had sizzle, the sexual tension was intense and at times heartwrenching and frustrating. I love every minute of it though, and when these two get together-they cause the earth to move. I kid you not, this book had some of the most erotic scenes in it that I have ever read. All, I will tell you about one scene in particular is that Grace screamed, "Ah Pizza!" ( You will have to read it yourself to find out what that is all about; but I guarantee you that it is origional!LOL)<br />The other pleasant surprise in this story was the band members, and Grace's friend Lea..The humor in this story is just great, and seeing how all of these friends interact with each other is highly entertaining! <br /><br />I don't want to share a lot of details of the book, because I don't want to give things away. I will say that this has been a series where I didn't hold my expectations high, and I will gladly admit that I was so very wrong. This is up there with some of my favorite's for sure.<br />Shane is a hero that took me awhile to melt my heart to; but he really pulls through, and his love for Grace is inspiring.<br /><br />"I will pick up every little broken piece of you, every single fucking piece, Grace, and for the rest of my fucking life I will put you back together..I'll make you whole again."<br /><br />"Don't cry, babe. Every damn tear I have seen that fell from those silver eyes broke my heart. This, right here with you is the closest that I'll ever come to heaven. That's all right by me, because you are my heaven, Grace."<br /><br />Christine Zolendz is an author I will be looking out for in the future. I love her style of writing, and her sense of humor shines through on the pages of her book. I can't wait to read the third book in this sexy series, as it is in Shane's POV. I have no doubt that it will be hot, and I will love it from start to finish! <br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8275845773620209025"><i>5+ stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"…the fairy-tale I’d write for you, Grace. You and Shane. One hot rock star badass and one beautiful rock star badass with a happily ever after"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535030i/4995188.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Waking up from a coma, she never expected to be saved and sent back to earth without her Angel. He left her to be free to live a life without him, completely broken Grace has to find a way to live a life as a mortal, but thousands of years is going to be hard to just forget and just LIVE. Could she put aside her love for her Angel and</span>
  <span id="freeText8275845773620209025" style="display:none"><i>5+ stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"…the fairy-tale I’d write for you, Grace. You and Shane. One hot rock star badass and one beautiful rock star badass with a happily ever after"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535030i/4995188.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Waking up from a coma, she never expected to be saved and sent back to earth without her Angel. He left her to be free to live a life without him, completely broken Grace has to find a way to live a life as a mortal, but thousands of years is going to be hard to just forget and just LIVE. Could she put aside her love for her Angel and find peace and love with the one man that made her almost forget about her Angel? <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No matter what happens from here , know that I have always, I will always love you and I will always protect you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535030i/4995189._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Grace struggles with facing the man who held her beloved Angel within him, she thinks back to the day when he professed his love for her, but now that her Angel is gone, they have to start all over. Who is Shane without the Angel, is he the same man that she could lose her self with? <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Centuries of being true and moral, I got my heart broken, then I meet Shane Maxton and I throw all my ethics out the window. I’m so going to enjoy this. I’m so not ever going to get to see my angel again in heaven, because I’m so going straight to hell. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Misunderstandings mixed in with their quick tempers get in the way of seeing where it all could lead, but their love hate relationship just gets stronger and stronger. They don't hesitate to bring out the big guns to drive each other wet or hard<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I could have had an orgasm from the mind fuck he was giving me right there.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Shane isn’t known for his relationships and commitments, but time and time he is there for Grace whenever she needs him most. Music is the one thing they always had in common, and it’s with music they can freely express themselves to each other.<br> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I wanted to tell you how I felt. Why I was always so mean to you, Shane.” <br><br>“Because you feel broken?” <br><br>“Completely shattered,” I whispered softly.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381535030ra/4995191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Shane and Grace have this inner battle that they are quickly loosing, to everyone else it is all so perfectly clear and they just need to open up and let each other in. Even in her new life she is still a prisoner from her of Gabriel, the first fallen angel who wants her all to himself, threatening and taunting her each chance he gets <b>
  <i>"The devil says he loves me, and he’s coming to get me."</i>
</b> Luckily she has true friends who love her and won’t let her get hurt, willing to be by her side every moment. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535030i/4995190._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I absolutely loved this book, the tension and the banter held my attention the entire way, perfectly content watching these two people navigate their way around each other. Shane was to die for, he is such a tortured hero and I loved everything about him, past and all. Grace is such a bad-ass, I loved her feistiness and her strength. Their friends are amazing and had me laughing right through all the drama. <br><br>It was a perfect mix, light on the paranormal, heavy on the sexual tension and big on the love. I'm still deciding if I'm gonna read Shane's POV, I have it on my kindle, but scared it's gonna change my view of Shane. We'll see how long I can hold out, but I'm jonesing for more of their story so I just might dive right in and hope for the best. </span>

  <span id="freeText2709755741427830501" style="display:none"><b>OH. MY! GOD!!</b><br>That was beyond perfection .. that was .. I have no words!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360599.gif" width="200" height="153" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394269ra/759116.gif" width="312" height="176" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Favorite quote:</b> <i>"Grace, I still have the taste of you on my tongue and the feel of your body in my arms, you're not easy to get off my mind. As a matter of fact, I haven't thought about anything else since I first laid my eyes on you."</i><br><br>I feel so happy right now, my life is complete!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394269ra/759117.gif" width="250" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Only three books have ever made me fangirl so much .. Beautiful Disaster, Fall From Grace AND Saving Grace. <br><br>My inner fangirl has been on overdrive for two days now ... because I have done nothing other than read Fall From Grace and Saving Grace for two whole days. My family think I'm crazy, and think I should spent som time in the real world .. and maybe stop screaming so much like a little girl ... and maybe actually start on the assignment that has to be done in a couple of days, buuut. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394269ra/759118.gif" width="450" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I liked that this book began right where the last one ended. <br><br>But I must say that I was reeeeally confused in the beginning .. actually I still am, so if any of you who have read the book can answer me this .. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[What is with the 'Shane situation'?<br>So her angel never left her? He was in Shane/was Shane? this whole time? And what? So Shane had a soul and her angel had a soul? And then they just shared the same body? Or had the angel been in the Shane body since he was born .. so that the angel actually was Shane? I don't get it! And I have cracked my brain trying to figure it out. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And I LOVED the characters!<br><br>Lea is so perfect! She is such a good friend, and so loyal .. and funny, I love her!<br><br><i>"Look, Gray...a decent guy doesn't just get born and grow up to be Mr. Perfect. They need to be created by a woman. They're like a dumb blank lump of clay and you have to mold them into what you want them to be, while erasing everything their mothers ever taught them and all the internet porn they've watched growing up."</i><br><br>And Grace, I loved her too. Even though she frustrated me too, but that was just because of all the love that she refused to acknowledge that was RIGHT IN FRONT OF HER!<br>But she was really funny too, and I liked reading the story from her point of view. <br><br><i>"That damn beautiful smirk that was on his face made me want to climb up his body and lick his lips."</i><br><b>I K N O W ! !</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/482407.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And Shane, whoooa! The perfect mix of sweet and caring and badass and hot as hell! <br><br>I so WANTED .. NEEDED Grace and Shane to get to the good stuff, and they kept getting interrupted and I kept getting more and more frustrated. So when they finally did, I totally freaked! It was the hottest thing .. ever!<br><br>I don't know how to do this book justice .. it was too good! <br>So .. I'll let it speak for itself: <br><br><i>"You two are making me feel like I need to wear a condom over my head so I can't get pregnant from just listening to the both of you."</i><br><br><i>"I know I'm drunk as hell, Grace, but, just stay with me. I need you like I fucking need to breathe."</i><br><br><i>“I want to be inside you so damn bad right now. But when I do that, I want to hear you scream my fucking name as you claw your nails down my back. <span id="freeTextContainer12030542676090894129"><b>Minor Spoilers</b> -Do not read if you have not read book one <br/>3 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: Paranormal Romance/Fantasy/Contemporary Romance<br/><i> <b><br/>'Holy Dripping Wet Panties! The one who captured her heart.<br/> When the b</span>
  <span id="freeText12030542676090894129" style="display:none"><b>Minor Spoilers</b> -Do not read if you have not read book one <br />3 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Paranormal Romance/Fantasy/Contemporary Romance<br /><i> <b><br />'Holy Dripping Wet Panties! That man should come with a warning label.'</b></i> ~Inner Monologue of Grace<br /><br />Yes. He. Should.<br /><br /> 2,000 years.... Could you imagine your soul going through time from one life to the next in search of it's soul mate? Well that is exactly what happened to Selah now known as Grace. And finally she has found him... The one who captured her heart.<br /> When the book starts her life hangs in the balance she discovers that the one she thought she could trust is nothing but a backstabbing infatuated stalker.<br /> Seriously, Gabriel drove me BATSH!T CRAZY. But I don't wanna talk about him... <br />I wanna talk about Shane. <br /><br />11/17/12 -Okay, so I'm a little conflicted on how to rate this... I liked it, I didn't love it. I did love Shane.<i> A LOT!</i> Can't put my finger on it so I will let the story digest for a few days. <br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><b>EDITED on 11/27/12</b><br /><br />Like I previously said, I wanna talk about Shane!<br />His character was very swoon worthy. And the attraction doubled once he gave up his man whore ways in book2. He was a total alpha male, very overprotective and would knock a guy on his ass for stepping to Grace. He played the guitar, sung lead in a band and had a sexy swagger. <br />Seriously, what's not to like?<br /><br /><u>Fave lines said and unsaid</u><br /><br /><i>'Oh my God. Perfection. He was utterly the most breathtaking, painfully beautiful man I had ever laid my eyes on.'</i> ~Internal monologue Grace<br /><br /><i>I just wanted to wrap my legs around his face.'</i> ~Internal monologue Grace <br /><br /><i>'I was speechless anyway. I couldn’t even think right. Well… mentally he was about eight inches deep in me and I was screaming his name raking my nails down his back.'</i> ~Internal monologue Grace<br /><br /><i>“Oh, my God, Grace. Shane is completely eye fucking you and I’m creaming in my panties right now. How does that not affect you?”</i> ~Lea<br /><br />Dear reader<br />I am no longer conflicted I decided to go with 3 SOLID STARS as a rating here is why.<br /><br /><b>The Story</b><br />I felt the story ended and left me with more questions. A lot of them. I also felt that the mythology used was not exactly original it had a few similarities that I read in another series. That series being <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6487308.Fallen__Fallen___1_" title="Fallen (Fallen, #1) by Lauren Kate" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen</a>. In all honesty it was only small similarities never the less still there.<br /><br />Also I don't understand why Shane allowed certain things to occur after... certain facts surfaced. On top of that I would have loved for Shane to explain some things. I found myself unfulfilled at the end of the book because I had questions that only his character could rectify. Better yet, if his pov played out along with Grace's it would have given readers a deeper understanding of just how epic their lovestory is. <br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Sexy, Witty and some were deceiving<br />Writing Style- Fair<br />Storyline/Plot- Okay<br />Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br />Overall- I liked it!!<br /><b><br />Now go forth and read. Then tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_429665919" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429665919" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429665919?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429665919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13406457622813254362"><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I love pop-tarts. I <i>really</i> love Lucky Charms. Who doesn't? They're magically delicious! But raise your hand if you like to pick off the brown edges of a pop-tart or eat all the brown charms first and save the marshmallowy goodness for last. Anybody?? Sometimes we have to pick off the not so good parts to get to the part we really want...the part that's left...the awesomeness.<br/><br/>I'm convinced that Christine Zolendz <i>is</i> walking potential. The concepts and ideas she has in her head are unique,</span>
  <span id="freeText13406457622813254362" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b><br /><br />I love pop-tarts. I <i>really</i> love Lucky Charms. Who doesn't? They're magically delicious! But raise your hand if you like to pick off the brown edges of a pop-tart or eat all the brown charms first and save the marshmallowy goodness for last. Anybody?? Sometimes we have to pick off the not so good parts to get to the part we really want...the part that's left...the awesomeness.<br /><br />I'm convinced that Christine Zolendz <i>is</i> walking potential. The concepts and ideas she has in her head are unique, addictive and could explode into some really great books, but the execution just isn't quite there yet. <i>Saving Grace</i> had all the right ingredients. It smelled good cooking, but the cake never rose and the cookies were a little burnt. Okay I'm really sorry. I must have eaten analogy for breakfast because I keep pooping them out, but I'll stop now...maybe!<br /><br />Here's what's real. I felt like somebody pushed the repeat button with the plot. Don't get me wrong...there were parts that definitely could use a <s>"do me over"</s> "do over" button, but it kept cycling through the same parts just in a different way. Some parts confused me (especially the beginning...maybe I'm just not that smart) and the paranormal didn't blend with the plot as well as it did in book one. It felt like two separate stories happening. <br /><br />Among the happenings, one thing the author <i>did</i> know how to execute was chemistry and sexual tension! There were several parts that definitely made me pop a moisty! There was also some GREAT one-liners! <br /><br />I honestly saw a truly amazing book hiding behind some poor edits and a struggled execution. Despite the brown edges, I'm glad I read this series. It gave me some great characters, a steamy unique plot and introduced me to a new author that I think has some amazing potential. I think she'll get there! In the mean time, I'll wait! READ ON!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13406457622813254362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_439558127" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/439558127" />
    <a title="R.E. Hunter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19358067-r-e-hunter"><img alt="R.E. Hunter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470168750p2/19358067.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/439558127?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="R.E. Hunter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="R.E. Hunter" href="/user/show/19358067-r-e-hunter">R.E. Hunter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439558127" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11025657385081285079">Okay. I really, really tried. I got through <i>Fall From Grace</i> and thought maybe it would all come together in <i>Saving Grace, </i>but I'm left feeling even more frustrated, and completely unsatisfied.<br/><br/>Once again, potential is the key word. This book, the last book, this <i>series</i>, had the capability of being great - knock you on your ass with an amazing romance and a paranormal twist that wrenches your heart out of your chest and has you really, truly believing in soulmates - great. But it just completely f</span>
  <span id="freeText11025657385081285079" style="display:none">Okay. I really, really tried. I got through <i>Fall From Grace</i> and thought maybe it would all come together in <i>Saving Grace, </i>but I'm left feeling even more frustrated, and completely unsatisfied.<br /><br />Once again, potential is the key word. This book, the last book, this <i>series</i>, had the capability of being great - knock you on your ass with an amazing romance and a paranormal twist that wrenches your heart out of your chest and has you really, truly believing in soulmates - great. But it just completely falls short and leaves so many unanswered questions...<br /><br />This review is probably going to sound like a repeat of my review for <i>Fall From Grace, </i>but then again, most of this book was a repeat of <i>Fall From Grace</i>. Maybe I missed something, maybe I just don't understand, but <i>really, </i>I just don't understand! At the risk of being overly vague and cryptic because I don't want to give anything away...the whole basis of the book made positively no sense after the story unfolded. It's like a huge part of the story arc is just missing or was completely glossed over to get the end result that we wanted.<br /><br /><i>Saving Grace</i> felt just like I was reading <i>Fall From Grace</i> all over again. Through the first half of the book I was beyond frustrated and wanted to pull my hair out. After a brief detour in the beginning of the book, which only served to create more questions instead of offer any answers, we are right back to where we started with Grace and Shane being terrible to each other and it makes <i>no sense whatsoever.</i> The back and forth between them was absolutely maddening.<br /><br />Once again, after a little more than halfway through the book, things start to pick up and the sexual tension between Grace and Shane is off the charts. It's amazing and just keeps on leaving you wanting more. The problem is, the <i>more</i> that we're really in search of doesn't actually happen until you're about 90% finished with the book. Then it's wrapped up into a nice little package with no real explanations or answers and a very short epilogue that, although is very "happy epilogue after," left me feeling like I missed out on so much.<br /><br />I loved Shane. I can't stress this enough. His character made these books worth it for me. He's the reason I wanted to keep reading. And I grew to love Grace. And I loved them together. By the end of the book I was definitely connected to these two and the connection to their love story is why that 3rd star is still hanging up there.<br /><br />I don't want this to be too negative. As much as it frustrated me, I still enjoyed the book. I just wanted so much more out of it. I know the author is writing a book from Shane's POV next and I will happily read it. I just hope there will be some more answers...<br /><br />Reviewed at <a href="http://thebooklistreviews.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">thebooklistreviews.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11025657385081285079" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_428852450" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/428852450" />
    <a title="CeCe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10480068-cece"><img alt="CeCe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551369180p2/10480068.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/428852450?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CeCe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CeCe" href="/user/show/10480068-cece">CeCe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer428852450" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11602992007261847499">I so wanted to love the book. I bought it the minute it came out. Saving Grace is the sequel to Fall from Grace. I thought Fall from Grace was so-so, but I saw the potential when Shane discovered who the true Grace was, but NO. Did the author even address that in Saving Grace?! Not sure.<br/><br/>The whole game of miscommunication and misunderstanding was played until the very end. I hate that!! You have to do more in the story for me than..."does he love me, does he not?" "I saw him look at that girl. so</span>
  <span id="freeText11602992007261847499" style="display:none">I so wanted to love the book. I bought it the minute it came out. Saving Grace is the sequel to Fall from Grace. I thought Fall from Grace was so-so, but I saw the potential when Shane discovered who the true Grace was, but NO. Did the author even address that in Saving Grace?! Not sure.<br /><br />The whole game of miscommunication and misunderstanding was played until the very end. I hate that!! You have to do more in the story for me than..."does he love me, does he not?" "I saw him look at that girl. so I know he does not love me." Blah, blah, blah. It got annoying. What happened at 77% in the book, should have happened at 21% of the book. Then I would have felt that I was being thrown a bone. I don't even need "steamy" scenes, but a good kiss or an understanding that we care or love eachother does it for me. However, Grace was always thinking that Shane was sleeping with other women. Or they would get interrupted right before a special moment. Did she not know that they were soul-mates????? It got old for me especially in the second book. I love tension in a story, but in the sequel, you have to stop teasing me non-stop. Give me something!!! The plot never really took off for me. Sure Gabriel showed up here and there, but I cared less for the characters at that point. <br /><br />The questions I always ask at the end of a book:<br />Did I skim? Yes<br />Did I want the book to end? Yes. When we love the book, we get disappointed the closer we get to the end. I wanted this to end.<br />Will/would I reread this book? No<br />Did I count the minutes until I was going to go back to reading this book? No. <br />Did I think about this book after I finished? Only that I was disappointed that I did not enjoy it.:(<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11602992007261847499" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_439879668" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/439879668" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/439879668?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439879668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1685056906777283184">SQUEEEEEEEEEEEEEE!!!!!!!!!! Loved the ending!!!!!!! <br/><br/>This story picks up where Fall from Grace left off. I'm not going to go into details, for those who haven't yet finished book one. I just want to say that this was a well put together conclusion to the story!! I will also say that I only left a star off my review because of the monotonous and forehead banging sexual tension that flew back and forth between Grace and Shane throughout this book. By the end... I thought about hurling myself off of</span>
  <span id="freeText1685056906777283184" style="display:none">SQUEEEEEEEEEEEEEE!!!!!!!!!! Loved the ending!!!!!!! <br><br>This story picks up where Fall from Grace left off. I'm not going to go into details, for those who haven't yet finished book one. I just want to say that this was a well put together conclusion to the story!! I will also say that I only left a star off my review because of the monotonous and forehead banging sexual tension that flew back and forth between Grace and Shane throughout this book. By the end... I thought about hurling myself off of a very tall building.... but then, the swoon set in and I was sated!!! So much drama though.... I love him... but is he sincere?..... I love him but what about all of the others?.... I love him but does he love me? I love him... but will Gabriel hurt him? It goes on and on... and I almost lost my mind!!! <br><br>The story was compelling though, and I had trouble putting it down. And Shane... OMG Shane was just exquisite!! And the steamy moments were numerous and explosive. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I told you matching sets are weapons of mass destruction."</i>
</b><br><br>And the quotes continue... and they are beautiful... and render a total heart melt down...<br><br>"Hear my soul speak. Of the very instant that I saw you, did my heart fly at your service," he whispered. "Shakespeare. The Tempest." I looked away again wanting to throw myself at him. "Words have no power to impress the mind without the exquisite horror of their reality." Poe."<br><br>"Remember tonight for it is the beginning of always," he whispered, Dante Alighieri, Shane?" "Shut up and go to sleep, Grace."<br><br>Every bit of this story was romantic. From Grace's history to her final HEA with Shane, aka Shamsiel! And what a lovely twist of reality the author wove in with Gabriel's long felt desires and punishment. It was a beautiful ending to a lovely romance that took two centuries to fulfill!!!<br><br><b>*****4.5 STARS*****<br><br>pics....<br><br>Grace Taylor...<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/Megan-Fox-Fit.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177923.jpg" alt="Megan Fox photo Megan-Fox-Fit.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Shane Maxton...<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/NickAyler_9675.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177924.jpg" alt="Nick Ayler photo NickAyler_9675.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Gabriel...<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/FRAN6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177925.jpg" alt=" photo FRAN6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Lea...<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/AmberHeard997.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177926._SY540_.jpg" alt="Amber Heard photo AmberHeard997.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Connor...<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/luke-guldan-3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177927.jpg" alt=" photo luke-guldan-3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer428957511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7297965301896279857">Saving Grace is the second book in the Mad World Series by Christine Zolendz and the follow up to Fall from Grace (Book #1) which I absolutely adored right down to the core of my soul. When I saw that Saving Grace was available from Amazon I went all psycho and scared the life out of my family when I woohoo'ed loudly and did the sitting dance...<br/><br/>If you thought Fall from Grace was one of the best books of 2012 (which I totally did) then you have another thing coming... Saving Grace completely tops</span>
  <span id="freeText7297965301896279857" style="display:none">Saving Grace is the second book in the Mad World Series by Christine Zolendz and the follow up to Fall from Grace (Book #1) which I absolutely adored right down to the core of my soul. When I saw that Saving Grace was available from Amazon I went all psycho and scared the life out of my family when I woohoo'ed loudly and did the sitting dance...<br><br>If you thought Fall from Grace was one of the best books of 2012 (which I totally did) then you have another thing coming... Saving Grace completely tops Fall from Grace... in fact it's totally off the charts awesome and I didn't once... not even for a second put it down. Did an all-nighter and when I woke up this morning reread the last 3 chapters again just to make sure that it wasn't all a dream.<br><br>With about 244 pages it's not a really long book and I'm mildly depressed about that. Could easily have eaten up so much more of Grace and Shane's story :)<br><br>Saving Grace takes off from where Fall from Grace ended (which was such a hanger I couldn't believe it was even legal to do that)... I love that there were no lost moments between Grace and Shane and that we were pulled right back into story. I loved that Christine Zolendz didn't waste time getting right into the action and she didn't bore me with rehashing scene's from Fall from Grace. I completely hate it when a second book spends half of it's pages telling us (who have already read it BTW) what happened in the first book. Argh it grinds me! BUT Christine didn't torture me with any of that nonsense and I thank her for that. Saving Grace began with guns blazing and my adrenaline spiked from the first page :)<br><br><div>
